    "appreg = r'href=\\\"(/store/apps/details.*?)\\\"'\n",
    "appre = re.compile(appreg)\n",
    "app_url_list = re.findall(appre,x)\n",
    "app_url_list = list(set(app_url_list))\n",
    "print(len(app_url_list))\n",
